# Humod_Torques

All codes presented here use data from https://www.sim.informatik.tu-darmstadt.de/res/ds/humod/ . However they can easily be adapted for other model or data

Codes present method and result to get the torques from a human biomechanical model of 30 degrees of freedom (DoF) + 6 DoF (virtual joint between the world and the pelvis)
